## Diagram 2

```mermaid
flowchart LR
    Start[Helm Template] --> Check{windows.enabled?}
    Check -->|No| End[Skip]
    Check -->|Yes| DS[Create DaemonSet]
    DS --> Meta[Set Metadata]
    Meta --> Spec[Define Spec]
    Spec --> Selector[Match Labels]
    Spec --> Strategy[Update Strategy]
    Spec --> Template[Pod Template]
    Template --> PodMeta[Pod Metadata]
    Template --> PodSpec[Pod Spec]
    PodSpec --> SA[ServiceAccount]
    PodSpec --> Affinity[Affinity Rules]
    PodSpec --> C1[node-driver-registrar]
    PodSpec --> C2[secrets-store]
    PodSpec --> C3{Version >= v0.0.9-0?}
    C3 -->|Yes| C4[liveness-probe]
    C3 -->|No| Skip1[Skip liveness-probe]
    PodSpec --> Vols[Volumes]
    PodSpec --> NS[Node Selector]
    PodSpec --> Tol[Tolerations]
```

## Diagram 3

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant Helm
    participant DaemonSet
    participant Node
    participant Registrar
    participant SecretsStore
    participant LivenessProbe

    Helm->>DaemonSet: Create if windows.enabled
    DaemonSet->>Node: Deploy to Windows nodes
    Node->>Registrar: Start node-driver-registrar
    Registrar->>Node: Register CSI driver
    Node->>SecretsStore: Start secrets-store container
    SecretsStore->>Node: Mount CSI socket
    SecretsStore->>Node: Configure environment
    alt Version >= v0.0.9-0
        Node->>LivenessProbe: Start liveness-probe
        LivenessProbe->>SecretsStore: Probe health
    end
    SecretsStore->>Node: Expose healthz port
    SecretsStore->>Node: Expose metrics port
```

## Diagram 4

```mermaid
classDiagram
    class DaemonSet {
        +kind: DaemonSet
        +apiVersion: apps/v1
        +metadata
        +spec
    }
    class Metadata {
        +name
        +namespace
        +labels
        +annotations
    }
    class Spec {
        +selector
        +updateStrategy
        +template
    }
    class PodTemplate {
        +metadata
        +spec
    }
    class PodSpec {
        +serviceAccountName
        +imagePullSecrets
        +affinity
        +containers[]
        +volumes[]
        +nodeSelector
        +tolerations[]
        +priorityClassName
    }
    class Container {
        +name
        +image
        +args[]
        +env[]
        +ports[]
        +volumeMounts[]
        +resources
        +livenessProbe
        +imagePullPolicy
    }
    class Volume {
        +name
        +hostPath
    }

    DaemonSet --> Metadata
    DaemonSet --> Spec
    Spec --> PodTemplate
    PodTemplate --> PodSpec
    PodSpec --> Container
    PodSpec --> Volume
```
